<t>CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS AI_models (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    model_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    model_accuracy FLOAT NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS AI_datasets (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    dataset_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    dataset_size INT NOT NULL,
    dataset_link VARCHAR(255)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS AI_users (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    role VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL
);</t><s>UPDATE AI_models SET model_accuracy = 0.85 WHERE model_name = 'Image Classifier';</s>

    username VARCHAR(255),

    role VARCHAR(50),

);
